12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter : This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not include the provider
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter : of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter : - You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a hot-reload.
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :   To fix, perform a hot-restart.
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter : - The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :   Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a route, then
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :   other routes will not be able to access that provider.
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter : - You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider you are trying to read.
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :   Make sure that _InheritedProviderScope<ChannelProvider?> is under your MultiProvider/Provider<EpgService>.
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :   This usually happens when you are creating a provider and trying to read it immediately.
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :   For example, instead of:
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```

12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :       // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is associated
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :       // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :       child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :     );
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :   }
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :   consider using `builder` like so:
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:45:03.664 29501 29501 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),

12-07 07:46:16.989 29501 29501 I flutter : Unhandled app error: Error: Could not find the correct Provider<EpgService> above this _InheritedProviderScope<ChannelProvider?> Widget
12-07 07:46:16.989 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:16.989 29501 29501 I flutter : This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not include the provider
12-07 07:46:16.989 29501 29501 I flutter : of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:
12-07 07:46:16.989 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:16.989 29501 29501 I flutter : - You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a hot-reload.
12-07 07:46:16.989 29501 29501 I flutter :   To fix, perform a hot-restart.
12-07 07:46:16.989 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:16.989 29501 29501 I flutter : - The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.
12-07 07:46:16.989 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:16.989 29501 29501 I flutter :   Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a route, then
12-07 07:46:16.989 29501 29501 I flutter :   other routes will not be able to access that provider.
12-07 07:46:16.989 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:16.989 29501 29501 I flutter : - You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider you are trying to read.
12-07 07:46:16.989 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:16.989 29501 29501 I flutter :   Make sure that _InheritedProviderScope<ChannelProvider?> is under your MultiProvider/Provider<EpgService>.
12-07 07:46:16.989 29501 29501 I flutter :   This usually happens when you are creating a provider and trying to read it immediately.
12-07 07:46:16.989 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:16.989 29501 29501 I flutter :   For example, instead of:
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :       // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is associated
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :       // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :       child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :     );
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :   }
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :   consider using `builder` like so:
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :       // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has access to the provider
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :       builder: (context, child) {
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :         // No longer throws
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :         return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :       }
12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :     );

12-07 07:46:16.990 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```

12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter : Unhandled app error: Error: Could not find the correct Provider<EpgService> above this _InheritedProviderScope<ChannelProvider?> Widget
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter : This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not include the provider
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter : of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter : - You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a hot-reload.
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :   To fix, perform a hot-restart.
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter : - The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :   Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a route, then
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :   other routes will not be able to access that provider.
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter : - You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider you are trying to read.
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :   Make sure that _InheritedProviderScope<ChannelProvider?> is under your MultiProvider/Provider<EpgService>.
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :   This usually happens when you are creating a provider and trying to read it immediately.
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :   For example, instead of:
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :       // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is associated
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :       // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :       child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :     );
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :   }
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :   consider using `builder` like so:
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :       // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has access to the provider
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :       builder: (context, child) {
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :         // No longer throws
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :         return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :       }
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :     );
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :   }
12-07 07:46:19.493 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```

12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter : Unhandled app error: Error: Could not find the correct Provider<EpgService> above this _InheritedProviderScope<ChannelProvider?> Widget
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter : This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not include the provider
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter : of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter : - You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a hot-reload.
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :   To fix, perform a hot-restart.
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter : - The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :   Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a route, then
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :   other routes will not be able to access that provider.
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter : - You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider you are trying to read.
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :   Make sure that _InheritedProviderScope<ChannelProvider?> is under your MultiProvider/Provider<EpgService>.
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :   This usually happens when you are creating a provider and trying to read it immediately.
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :   For example, instead of:
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :       // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is associated
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :       // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :       child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :     );
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :   }
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :   consider using `builder` like so:
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :       // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has access to the provider
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :       builder: (context, child) {
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :         // No longer throws
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :         return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :       }
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :     );
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :   }
12-07 07:46:21.513 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```

12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter : Unhandled app error: Error: Could not find the correct Provider<EpgService> above this _InheritedProviderScope<ChannelProvider?> Widget
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter : This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not include the provider
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter : of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter : - You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a hot-reload.
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :   To fix, perform a hot-restart.
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter : - The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :   Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a route, then
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :   other routes will not be able to access that provider.
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter : - You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider you are trying to read.
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :   Make sure that _InheritedProviderScope<ChannelProvider?> is under your MultiProvider/Provider<EpgService>.
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :   This usually happens when you are creating a provider and trying to read it immediately.
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :   For example, instead of:
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :       // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is associated
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :       // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :       child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :     );
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :   }
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :   consider using `builder` like so:
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :       // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has access to the provider
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :       builder: (context, child) {
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :         // No longer throws
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :         return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :       }
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :     );
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :   }
12-07 07:46:23.550 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```

12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter : Unhandled app error: Error: Could not find the correct Provider<EpgService> above this _InheritedProviderScope<ChannelProvider?> Widget
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter : This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not include the provider
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter : of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter : - You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a hot-reload.
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :   To fix, perform a hot-restart.
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter : - The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :   Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a route, then
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :   other routes will not be able to access that provider.
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter : - You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider you are trying to read.
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :   Make sure that _InheritedProviderScope<ChannelProvider?> is under your MultiProvider/Provider<EpgService>.
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :   This usually happens when you are creating a provider and trying to read it immediately.
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :   For example, instead of:
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :       // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is associated
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :       // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :       child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :     );
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :   }
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :   consider using `builder` like so:
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :       // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has access to the provider
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :       builder: (context, child) {
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :         // No longer throws
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :         return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :       }
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :     );
12-07 07:46:26.317 29501 29501 I flutter :   }

12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter : Unhandled app error: Error: Could not find the correct Provider<EpgService> above this _InheritedProviderScope<ChannelProvider?> Widget
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter : This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not include the provider
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter : of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter : - You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a hot-reload.
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :   To fix, perform a hot-restart.
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter : - The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :   Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a route, then
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :   other routes will not be able to access that provider.
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter : - You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider you are trying to read.
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :   Make sure that _InheritedProviderScope<ChannelProvider?> is under your MultiProvider/Provider<EpgService>.
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :   This usually happens when you are creating a provider and trying to read it immediately.
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :   For example, instead of:
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :       // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is associated
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :       // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :       child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :     );
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :   }
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :   consider using `builder` like so:
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :       // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has access to the provider
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :       builder: (context, child) {
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :         // No longer throws
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :         return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :       }
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :     );
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :   }
12-07 07:46:29.351 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```

12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter : Unhandled app error: Error: Could not find the correct Provider<EpgService> above this _InheritedProviderScope<ChannelProvider?> Widget
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter : This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not include the provider
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter : of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter : - You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a hot-reload.
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :   To fix, perform a hot-restart.
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter : - The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :   Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a route, then
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :   other routes will not be able to access that provider.
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter : - You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider you are trying to read.
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :   Make sure that _InheritedProviderScope<ChannelProvider?> is under your MultiProvider/Provider<EpgService>.
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :   This usually happens when you are creating a provider and trying to read it immediately.
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :   For example, instead of:
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :       // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is associated
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :       // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :       child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :     );
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :   }
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :   consider using `builder` like so:
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :       // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has access to the provider
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :       builder: (context, child) {
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :         // No longer throws
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :         return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :       }
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :     );
12-07 07:46:31.601 29501 29501 I flutter :   }
12-07 07:46:31.602 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```

12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :       // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is associated
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :       // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :       child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :     );
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :   }
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :   consider using `builder` like so:
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter : 
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :       // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has access to the provider
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :       builder: (context, child) {
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :         // No longer throws
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :         return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :       }
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :     );
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :   }
12-07 07:47:03.828 29501 29501 I flutter :   ```

12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter : Unhandled app error: Error: Could not find the correct Provider<EpgService> above this _InheritedProviderScope<ChannelProvider?> Widget
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter : 
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter : This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not include the provider
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter : of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter : 
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter : - You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a hot-reload.
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :   To fix, perform a hot-restart.
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter : 
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter : - The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter : 
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :   Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a route, then
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :   other routes will not be able to access that provider.
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter : 
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter : - You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider you are trying to read.
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter : 
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :   Make sure that _InheritedProviderScope<ChannelProvider?> is under your MultiProvider/Provider<EpgService>.
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :   This usually happens when you are creating a provider and trying to read it immediately.
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter : 
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :   For example, instead of:
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter : 
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :       // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is associated
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :       // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :       child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :     );
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :   }
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter : 
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :   consider using `builder` like so:
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter : 
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :   ```
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :     return Provider<Example>(
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :       create: (_) => Example(),
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :       // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has access to the provider
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :       builder: (context, child) {
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :         // No longer throws
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :         return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :       }
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :     );
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :   }
12-07 07:58:10.811 11149 11149 I flutter :   ```
